\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.26 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{                                  no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{   Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{      \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{   before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{   // i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{   \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{   You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{   And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{   QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{      Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{          avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{      JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{      PNG 1/2/4/8/16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{      TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{      BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{      PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{      GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{      HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{      PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{      PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{      Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{          http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{   Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'desired\_channels' if desired\_channels is non-\/zero, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file otherwise. If desired\_channels is non-\/zero,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file has the number of components that \_would\_ have been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{// output otherwise. E.g. if you set desired\_channels to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *channels\_in\_file to see if it's trivially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{// opaque because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *channels\_in\_file will be unchanged. The function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_failure\_reason() can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{// unfriendly explanation of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{// to avoid compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{// UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{//   If compiling for Windows and you wish to use Unicode filenames, compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{//   with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{//       \#define STBI\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//   and pass utf8-\/encoded filenames. Call stbi\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8 to convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{//   Windows wchar\_t filenames to utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy-\/to-\/use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries DO NOT emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{// provide more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small source code footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image supports loading HDR images in general, and currently the Radiance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{// .HDR file format specifically. You can still load any file through the existing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{// interface; if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{// to LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{// By default we convert iphone-\/formatted PNGs back to RGB, even though}}
\DoxyCodeLine{285 \textcolor{comment}{// they are internally encoded differently. You can disable this conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{286 \textcolor{comment}{// by calling stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0), in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287 \textcolor{comment}{// you will always just get the native iphone "{}format"{} through (which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288 \textcolor{comment}{// is BGR stored in RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{289 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{290 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{291 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{292 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{293 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{294 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{295 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{296 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{297 \textcolor{comment}{// ADDITIONAL CONFIGURATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{298 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{299 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can suppress implementation of any of the decoders to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{300 \textcolor{comment}{//    your code footprint by \#defining one or more of the following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{301 \textcolor{comment}{//    symbols before creating the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{302 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{303 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{304 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{305 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{306 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{307 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{308 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{309 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{310 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{311 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_NO\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{312 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{313 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can request *only* certain decoders and suppress all other ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{314 \textcolor{comment}{//    (this will be more forward-\/compatible, as addition of new decoders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315 \textcolor{comment}{//    doesn't require you to disable them explicitly):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_TGA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_GIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_HDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325 \textcolor{comment}{//        STBI\_ONLY\_PNM   (.ppm and .pgm)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ If you use STBI\_NO\_PNG (or \_ONLY\_ without PNG), and you still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 \textcolor{comment}{//     want the zlib decoder to be available, \#define STBI\_SUPPORT\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If you define STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS, stb\_image will reject images greater}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331 \textcolor{comment}{//    than that size (in either width or height) without further processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332 \textcolor{comment}{//    This is to let programs in the wild set an upper bound to prevent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333 \textcolor{comment}{//    denial-\/of-\/service attacks on untrusted data, as one could generate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 \textcolor{comment}{//    valid image of gigantic dimensions and force stb\_image to allocate a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335 \textcolor{comment}{//    huge block of memory and spend disproportionate time decoding it. By}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336 \textcolor{comment}{//    default this is set to (1 << 24), which is 16777216, but that's still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337 \textcolor{comment}{//    very big.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{338 }

\DoxyCodeLine{665 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{666 \textcolor{comment}{// gcc doesn't support sse2 intrinsics unless you compile with -\/msse2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{667 \textcolor{comment}{// which in turn means it gets to use SSE2 everywhere. This is unfortunate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{668 \textcolor{comment}{// but previous attempts to provide the SSE2 functions with runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{669 \textcolor{comment}{// detection caused numerous issues. The way architecture extensions are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{670 \textcolor{comment}{// exposed in GCC/Clang is, sadly, not really suited for one-\/file libs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{671 \textcolor{comment}{// New behavior: if compiled with -\/msse2, we use SSE2 without any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672 \textcolor{comment}{// detection; if not, we don't use it at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675 }
\DoxyCodeLine{676 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{687 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690 }

\DoxyCodeLine{850 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_rewind(stbi\_\_context* s)}

\DoxyCodeLine{852     \textcolor{comment}{// conceptually rewind SHOULD rewind to the beginning of the stream,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{853     \textcolor{comment}{// but we just rewind to the beginning of the initial buffer, because}}

\DoxyCodeLine{948 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_malloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{949 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{950     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_MALLOC(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{951 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{953 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{954 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{955 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{956 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{957 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{958 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{959 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{960 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{961 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{963 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{966 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{967     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{968     \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{969     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970     \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971     \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{972     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{973 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{974 }
\DoxyCodeLine{975 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{976 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{977 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{978 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{979     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{980     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{981     \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{982     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX / b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{983 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{985 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(STBI\_NO\_JPEG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_PNG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_TGA) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{986 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if "{}a*b + add"{} has no negative terms/factors and doesn't overflow}}

\DoxyCodeLine{988 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{989     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(a, b) \&\& stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(a * b, add);}

\DoxyCodeLine{991 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1162 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_vertical\_flip(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* image, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bytes\_per\_pixel)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_per\_row = (size\_t)w * bytes\_per\_pixel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166     stbi\_uc temp[2048];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167     stbi\_uc* bytes = (stbi\_uc*)image;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1169     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (row = 0; row < (h >> 1); row++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170         stbi\_uc* row0 = bytes + row * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171         stbi\_uc* row1 = bytes + (h -\/ row -\/ 1) * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172         \textcolor{comment}{// swap row0 with row1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_left = bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (bytes\_left) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_copy = (bytes\_left < \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp)) ? bytes\_left : \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176             memcpy(temp, row0, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177             memcpy(row0, row1, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178             memcpy(row1, temp, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179             row0 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180             row1 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1181             bytes\_left -\/= bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1854 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}baseline"{} JPEG/JFIF decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1857 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1859 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1860 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1861 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1862 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1863 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1864 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1865 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1867 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1868 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1871 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1872 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1873 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1874 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1876 \textcolor{comment}{// huffman decoding acceleration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FAST\_BITS   9  }\textcolor{comment}{// larger handles more cases; smaller stomps less cache}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1878 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1879 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881     stbi\_uc  fast[1 << FAST\_BITS];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882     \textcolor{comment}{// weirdly, repacking this into AoS is a 10\% speed loss, instead of a win}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883     stbi\_\_uint16 code[256];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884     stbi\_uc  values[256];}

\DoxyCodeLine{1944 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman* h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1945 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1946     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1947     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1948     \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1949     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1950         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1951             h-\/>size[k++] = (stbi\_uc)(i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1952     h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1953 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1954     \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1955     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1956     k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1957     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1958         \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1959         h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1960         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1961             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1962                 h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1u << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1965         \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966         h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16 -\/ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1967         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1968     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969     h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1971     \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1972     memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1973     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1974         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1975         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1976             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1977             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1978             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1979                 h-\/>fast[c + j] = (stbi\_uc)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1980             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1981         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1982     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1983     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1984 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1985 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1986 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1987 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1988 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16* fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman* h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1989 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1990     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1992         stbi\_uc fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1993         fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1994         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1995             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1996             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1997             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1998             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1999 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2000             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2001                 \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2002                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2003                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2004                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (\string~0U << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2005                 \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2006                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2007                     fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16)((k * 256) + (run * 16) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2008             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2009         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2010     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2011 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2012 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2013 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2015     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = j-\/>nomore ? 0 : stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0xff) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2018             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2019             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (c == 0xff) c = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021                 j-\/>marker = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022                 j-\/>nomore = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026         j-\/>code\_buffer |= b << (24 -\/ j-\/>code\_bits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027         j-\/>code\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (j-\/>code\_bits <= 24);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2031 \textcolor{comment}{// (1 << n) -\/ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_\_uint32 stbi\_\_bmask[17] = \{ 0,1,3,7,15,31,63,127,255,511,1023,2047,4095,8191,16383,32767,65535 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{2034 \textcolor{comment}{// decode a jpeg huffman value from the bitstream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(stbi\_\_jpeg* j, stbi\_\_huffman* h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2040     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2042     \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043     \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044     c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS))\& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045     k = h-\/>fast[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050         j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2052         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2055     \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2056     \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057     \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2058     \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2059     \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2060     \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061     temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = FAST\_BITS + 1; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2064             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066         \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2068         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2071     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2074     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075     c = ((j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ k))\& stbi\_\_bmask[k]) + h-\/>delta[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076     STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c]))\& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2078     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079     j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080     j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2081     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2083 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2084 \textcolor{comment}{// bias[n] = (-\/1<<n) + 1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2126 \textcolor{comment}{// given a value that's at position X in the zigzag stream,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2143 \textcolor{comment}{// decode one 64-\/entry block-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2144 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(stbi\_\_jpeg* j, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64], stbi\_\_huffman* hdc, stbi\_\_huffman* hac, stbi\_\_int16* fac, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b, stbi\_\_uint16* dequant)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2145 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2146     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} diff, dc, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2147     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2148 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2149     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2150     t = stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(j, hdc);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2151     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (t < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad huffman code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{2152 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2153     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 all the ac values now so we can do it 32-\/bits at a time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2154     memset(data, 0, 64 * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(data[0]));}
\DoxyCodeLine{2155 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2156     diff = t ? stbi\_\_extend\_receive(j, t) : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2157     dc = j-\/>img\_comp[b].dc\_pred + diff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2158     j-\/>img\_comp[b].dc\_pred = dc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2159     data[0] = (short)(dc * dequant[0]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2160 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2161     \textcolor{comment}{// decode AC components, see JPEG spec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2162     k = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2163     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2164         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} zig;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2165         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, r, s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2166         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2167         c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS))\& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2168         r = fac[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2169         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/AC path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2170             k += (r >> 4) \& 15; \textcolor{comment}{// run}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2171             s = r \& 15; \textcolor{comment}{// combined length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2172             j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2173             j-\/>code\_bits -\/= s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2174             \textcolor{comment}{// decode into unzigzag'd location}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2175             zig = stbi\_\_jpeg\_dezigzag[k++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2176             data[zig] = (short)((r >> 8)* dequant[zig]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2177         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2178         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2179             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = stbi\_\_jpeg\_huff\_decode(j, hac);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2180             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rs < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad huffman code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{2181             s = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2182             r = rs >> 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2183             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2184                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rs != 0xf0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \textcolor{comment}{// end block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2185                 k += 16;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2195     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2405 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_block(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2406 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2407     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, val[64], * v = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2408     stbi\_uc* o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2409     \textcolor{keywordtype}{short}* d = data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2410 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2411     \textcolor{comment}{// columns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2412     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 8; ++i, ++d, ++v) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2413         \textcolor{comment}{// if all zeroes, shortcut -\/-\/ this avoids dequantizing 0s and IDCTing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2414         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d[8] == 0 \&\& d[16] == 0 \&\& d[24] == 0 \&\& d[32] == 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2415             \&\& d[40] == 0 \&\& d[48] == 0 \&\& d[56] == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2416             \textcolor{comment}{//    no shortcut                 0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2417             \textcolor{comment}{//    (1|2|3|4|5|6|7)==0          0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2418             \textcolor{comment}{//    all separate               -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2419             \textcolor{comment}{//    1 \&\& 2|3 \&\& 4|5 \&\& 6|7:    -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2420             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dcterm = d[0] * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2421             v[0] = v[8] = v[16] = v[24] = v[32] = v[40] = v[48] = v[56] = dcterm;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2422         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424             STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(d[0], d[8], d[16], d[24], d[32], d[40], d[48], d[56])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425                 \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426                 \textcolor{comment}{// down, but keep 2 extra bits of precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427                 x0 += 512; x1 += 512; x2 += 512; x3 += 512;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428             v[0] = (x0 + t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429             v[56] = (x0 -\/ t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430             v[8] = (x1 + t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431             v[48] = (x1 -\/ t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432             v[16] = (x2 + t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433             v[40] = (x2 -\/ t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434             v[24] = (x3 + t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435             v[32] = (x3 -\/ t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2439     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0, v = val, o = out; i < 8; ++i, v += 8, o += out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440         \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441         STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3], v[4], v[5], v[6], v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442             \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443             \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444             \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445             \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446             \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447             \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448             x0 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449         x1 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450         x2 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451         x3 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452         \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453         \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454         o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 + t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455         o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 -\/ t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2456         o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 + t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457         o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 -\/ t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458         o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 + t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459         o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 -\/ t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460         o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 + t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461         o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 -\/ t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2462     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2463 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2465 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466 \textcolor{comment}{// sse2 integer IDCT. not the fastest possible implementation but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467 \textcolor{comment}{// produces bit-\/identical results to the generic C version so it's}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2854 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_MARKER\_none  0xff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855 \textcolor{comment}{// if there's a pending marker from the entropy stream, return that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise, fetch from the stream and get a marker. if there's no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857 \textcolor{comment}{// marker, return 0xff, which is never a valid marker value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2858 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc stbi\_\_get\_marker(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2860     stbi\_uc x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>marker != STBI\_\_MARKER\_none) \{ x = j-\/>marker; j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2862     x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2863     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x != 0xff) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (x == 0xff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2865         x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume repeated 0xff fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2867 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2868 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2869 \textcolor{comment}{// in each scan, we'll have scan\_n components, and the order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2870 \textcolor{comment}{// of the components is specified by order[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2871 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_RESTART(x)     ((x) >= 0xd0 \&\& (x) <= 0xd7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2872 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2873 \textcolor{comment}{// after a restart interval, stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset the entropy decoder and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874 \textcolor{comment}{// the dc prediction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2875 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877     j-\/>code\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2878     j-\/>code\_buffer = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2879     j-\/>nomore = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2880     j-\/>img\_comp[0].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[1].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[2].dc\_pred = j-\/>img\_comp[3].dc\_pred = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881     j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882     j-\/>todo = j-\/>restart\_interval ? j-\/>restart\_interval : 0x7fffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883     j-\/>eob\_run = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884     \textcolor{comment}{// no more than 1<<31 MCUs if no restart\_interal? that's plenty safe,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885     \textcolor{comment}{// since we don't even allow 1<<30 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2888 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_parse\_entropy\_coded\_data(stbi\_\_jpeg* z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2890     stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!z-\/>progressive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>scan\_n == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896             \textcolor{comment}{// non-\/interleaved data, we just need to process one block at a time,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897             \textcolor{comment}{// in trivial scanline order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898             \textcolor{comment}{// number of blocks to do just depends on how many actual "{}pixels"{} this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2899             \textcolor{comment}{// component has, independent of interleaved MCU blocking and such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2900             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].x + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].y + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < h; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ha = z-\/>img\_comp[n].ha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(z, data, z-\/>huff\_dc + z-\/>img\_comp[n].hd, z-\/>huff\_ac + ha, z-\/>fast\_ac[ha], n, z-\/>dequant[z-\/>img\_comp[n].tq])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906                     z-\/>idct\_block\_kernel(z-\/>img\_comp[n].data + z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2 * j * 8 + i * 8, z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2, data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907                     \textcolor{comment}{// every data block is an MCU, so countdown the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910                         \textcolor{comment}{// if it's NOT a restart, then just bail, so we get corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911                         \textcolor{comment}{// rather than no data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBI\_\_RESTART(z-\/>marker)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913                         stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{ \textcolor{comment}{// interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k, x, y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2922             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < z-\/>img\_mcu\_y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2923                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < z-\/>img\_mcu\_x; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2924                     \textcolor{comment}{// scan an interleaved mcu... process scan\_n components in order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2925                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = 0; k < z-\/>scan\_n; ++k) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2926                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2927                         \textcolor{comment}{// scan out an mcu's worth of this component; that's just determined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2928                         \textcolor{comment}{// by the basic H and V specified for the component}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2929                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (y = 0; y < z-\/>img\_comp[n].v; ++y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2930                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = 0; x < z-\/>img\_comp[n].h; ++x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2931                                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x2 = (i * z-\/>img\_comp[n].h + x) * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2932                                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y2 = (j * z-\/>img\_comp[n].v + y) * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933                                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ha = z-\/>img\_comp[n].ha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(z, data, z-\/>huff\_dc + z-\/>img\_comp[n].hd, z-\/>huff\_ac + ha, z-\/>fast\_ac[ha], n, z-\/>dequant[z-\/>img\_comp[n].tq])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2935                                 z-\/>idct\_block\_kernel(z-\/>img\_comp[n].data + z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2 * y2 + x2, z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2, data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2936                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2937                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2938                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2939                     \textcolor{comment}{// after all interleaved components, that's an interleaved MCU,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2940                     \textcolor{comment}{// so now count down the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBI\_\_RESTART(z-\/>marker)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944                         stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2945                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2946                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2947             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3453     \textcolor{comment}{// need to generate 2x2 samples for every one in input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0, t0, t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3456     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457         out[0] = out[1] = stbi\_\_div4(3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3461     t1 = 3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462     \textcolor{comment}{// process groups of 8 pixels for as long as we can.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463     \textcolor{comment}{// note we can't handle the last pixel in a row in this loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464     \textcolor{comment}{// because we need to handle the filter boundary conditions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < ((w -\/ 1) \& \string~7); i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469         \_\_m128i zero = \_mm\_setzero\_si128();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470         \_\_m128i farb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_far + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471         \_\_m128i nearb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_near + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472         \_\_m128i farw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473         \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474         \_\_m128i diff = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475         \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476         \_\_m128i curr = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3478         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483         \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484         \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485         \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486         \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3488         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492         \_\_m128i bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493         \_\_m128i curs = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494         \_\_m128i prvd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495         \_\_m128i nxtd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496         \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497         \_\_m128i even = \_mm\_add\_epi16(prvd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498         \_\_m128i odd = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3500         \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501         \_\_m128i int0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         \_\_m128i int1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503         \_\_m128i de0 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int0, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504         \_\_m128i de1 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int1, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3506         \textcolor{comment}{// pack and write output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507         \_\_m128i outv = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(de0, de1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508         \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + i * 2), outv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512         uint8x8\_t farb = vld1\_u8(in\_far + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513         uint8x8\_t nearb = vld1\_u8(in\_near + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514         int16x8\_t diff = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vsubl\_u8(farb, nearb));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515         int16x8\_t nears = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(nearb, 2));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516         int16x8\_t curr = vaddq\_s16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3518         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523         int16x8\_t prv0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524         int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525         int16x8\_t prev = vsetq\_lane\_s16(t1, prv0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526         int16x8\_t next = vsetq\_lane\_s16(3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], nxt0, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3528         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532         int16x8\_t curs = vshlq\_n\_s16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533         int16x8\_t prvd = vsubq\_s16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534         int16x8\_t nxtd = vsubq\_s16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535         int16x8\_t even = vaddq\_s16(curs, prvd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536         int16x8\_t odd = vaddq\_s16(curs, nxtd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3538         \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling and round, then store with even/odd phases interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539         uint8x8x2\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540         o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(even, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541         o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542         vst2\_u8(out + i * 2, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3545         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}previous"{} value for next iter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i + 7] + in\_far[i + 7];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3549     t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550     t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551     out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3552 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3553     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (++i; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3554         t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556         out[i * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t0 + t1 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557         out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559     out[w * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3560 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3561     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3562 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3563     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3564 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3565 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3567 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_generic(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3568 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3569     \textcolor{comment}{// resample with nearest-\/neighbor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571     STBI\_NOTUSED(in\_far);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3573         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < hs; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574             out[i * hs + j] = in\_near[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3577 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3578 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579 \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure the code produces the same results in both SIMD and scalar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3582 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3583     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3584     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3585         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3587         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589         r = y\_fixed + cr * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3590         g = y\_fixed + (cr * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f)) + ((cb * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3591         b = y\_fixed + cb * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3594         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3595         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3597         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3603     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3606 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* y, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcb, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3611 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612     \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613     \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614     \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617         \_\_m128i signflip = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618         \_\_m128i cr\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619         \_\_m128i cr\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620         \_\_m128i cb\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621         \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622         \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623         \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3625         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627             \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (y + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628             \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcr + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629             \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcb + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630             \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631             \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3633             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634             \_\_m128i yw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635             \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3636             \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3638             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3639             \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3640             \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641             \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642             \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3643             \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644             \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645             \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646             \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647             \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3649             \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650             \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651             \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3652             \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3654             \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655             \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656             \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3658             \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659             \_\_m128i t0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660             \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661             \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662             \_\_m128i o1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3664             \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 0), o0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667             out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3672 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673     \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676         uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677         int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678         int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679         int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680         int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3682         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684             uint8x8\_t y\_bytes = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685             uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686             uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687             int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688             int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3690             \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691             int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692             int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693             int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3695             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696             int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697             int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698             int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699             int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700             int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701             int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702             int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3704             \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705             uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706             o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707             o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708             o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3718     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4001 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4005 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4008 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4009 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4010 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4011 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4012 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4013 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4014 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4026 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4027 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4028     n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >> 1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4029     n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >> 2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4030     n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >> 4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4031     n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >> 8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4032     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4033 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4036 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037     STBI\_ASSERT(bits <= 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4038     \textcolor{comment}{// to bit reverse n bits, reverse 16 and shift}}
