\DoxyCodeLine{4043 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_zbuild\_huffman(stbi\_\_zhuffman* z, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* sizelist, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4044 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4045     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4046     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code, next\_code[16], sizes[17];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4047 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4048     \textcolor{comment}{// DEFLATE spec for generating codes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4049     memset(sizes, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(sizes));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4050     memset(z-\/>fast, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(z-\/>fast));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4051     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < num; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4052         ++sizes[sizelist[i]];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4053     sizes[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4054     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4055         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sizes[i] > (1 << i))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4056             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad sizes"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4057     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4058     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 1; i < 16; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059         next\_code[i] = code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060         z-\/>firstcode[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061         z-\/>firstsymbol[i] = (stbi\_\_uint16)k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4062         code = (code + sizes[i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4063         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (sizes[i])}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1 << i)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad codelengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4065         z-\/>maxcode[i] = code << (16 -\/ i); \textcolor{comment}{// preshift for inner loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067         k += sizes[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069     z-\/>maxcode[16] = 0x10000; \textcolor{comment}{// sentinel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < num; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4071         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = sizelist[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4072         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4073             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = next\_code[s] -\/ z-\/>firstcode[s] + z-\/>firstsymbol[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4074             stbi\_\_uint16 fastv = (stbi\_\_uint16)((s << 9) | i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075             z-\/>size[c] = (stbi\_uc)s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076             z-\/>value[c] = (stbi\_\_uint16)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4077             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4078                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} j = stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(next\_code[s], s);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4080                     z-\/>fast[j] = fastv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4081                     j += (1 << s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4082                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4083             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4084             ++next\_code[s];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4085         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4086     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4087     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4313 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_parse\_uncompressed\_block(stbi\_\_zbuf* a)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4314 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4315     stbi\_uc header[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4316     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len, nlen, k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4317     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a-\/>num\_bits \& 7)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4321     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (a-\/>num\_bits > 0) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4324         a-\/>num\_bits -\/= 8;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4326     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a-\/>num\_bits < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}zlib corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4331     nlen = header[3] * 256 + header[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4332     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (nlen != (len \string^ 0xffff)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}zlib corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PNG"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4334     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a-\/>zout + len > a-\/>zout\_end)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4335         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_zexpand(a, a-\/>zout, len)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4336     memcpy(a-\/>zout, a-\/>zbuffer, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4337     a-\/>zbuffer += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4338     a-\/>zout += len;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4505 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4506 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4507 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4508 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4509 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4510 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4511 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids explicit window management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4512 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4513 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses stb\_zlib, a PD zlib implementation with fast huffman decoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4514 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4515 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_PNG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4516 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4517 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4518     stbi\_\_uint32 length;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4519     stbi\_\_uint32 type;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4708     \textcolor{comment}{// we make a separate pass to expand bits to pixels; for performance,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4711     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4713             stbi\_uc* cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4715             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack 1/2/4-\/bit into a 8-\/bit buffer. allows us to keep the common 8-\/bit path optimal at minimal cost for 1/2/4-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716             \textcolor{comment}{// png guarante byte alignment, if width is not multiple of 8/4/2 we'll decode dummy trailing data that will be skipped in the later loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717             stbi\_uc scale = (color == 0) ? stbi\_\_depth\_scale\_table[depth] : 1; \textcolor{comment}{// scale grayscale values to 0..255 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4719             \textcolor{comment}{// note that the final byte might overshoot and write more data than desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720             \textcolor{comment}{// we can allocate enough data that this never writes out of memory, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721             \textcolor{comment}{// could also overwrite the next scanline. can it overwrite non-\/empty data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722             \textcolor{comment}{// on the next scanline? yes, consider 1-\/pixel-\/wide scanlines with 1-\/bit-\/per-\/pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723             \textcolor{comment}{// so we need to explicitly clamp the final ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4724 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4784     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4791 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5282 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 0..31 for the highest set bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5283 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_high\_bit(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5284 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5285     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5286     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5287     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x10000) \{ n += 16; z >>= 16; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5288     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00100) \{ n += 8; z >>= 8; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5289     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00010) \{ n += 4; z >>= 4; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5290     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00004) \{ n += 2; z >>= 2; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5291     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z >= 0x00002) \{ n += 1;\textcolor{comment}{/* >>=  1;*/} \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5292     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5293 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5295 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitcount(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5296 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5297     a = (a \& 0x55555555) + ((a >> 1) \& 0x55555555); \textcolor{comment}{// max 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5298     a = (a \& 0x33333333) + ((a >> 2) \& 0x33333333); \textcolor{comment}{// max 4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5299     a = (a + (a >> 4)) \& 0x0f0f0f0f; \textcolor{comment}{// max 8 per 4, now 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5300     a = (a + (a >> 8)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 16 per 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5301     a = (a + (a >> 16)); \textcolor{comment}{// max 32 per 8 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5302     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a \& 0xff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5303 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5743 \textcolor{comment}{// read 16bit value and convert to 24bit RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5744 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* out)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5745 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5746     stbi\_\_uint16 px = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5747     stbi\_\_uint16 fiveBitMask = 31;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5748     \textcolor{comment}{// we have 3 channels with 5bits each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5749     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (px >> 10)\& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5750     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} g = (px >> 5)\& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5751     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = px \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5752     \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this saves the data in RGB(A) order, so it doesn't need to be swapped later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5753     out[0] = (stbi\_uc)((r * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5754     out[1] = (stbi\_uc)((g * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5755     out[2] = (stbi\_uc)((b * 255) / 31);}

\DoxyCodeLine{5757     \textcolor{comment}{// some people claim that the most significant bit might be used for alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5758     \textcolor{comment}{// (possibly if an alpha-\/bit is set in the "{}image descriptor byte"{})}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5827             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} row = tga\_inverted ? tga\_height -\/ i -\/ 1 : i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5828             stbi\_uc* tga\_row = tga\_data + row * tga\_width * tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5829             stbi\_\_getn(s, tga\_row, tga\_width * tga\_comp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5830         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5831     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5832     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5833         \textcolor{comment}{//   do I need to load a palette?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5834         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_indexed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5835         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5836             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_palette\_len == 0) \{  \textcolor{comment}{/* you have to have at least one entry! */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5837                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5838                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad palette"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt TGA"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5839             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5840 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5841             \textcolor{comment}{//   any data to skip? (offset usually = 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5842             stbi\_\_skip(s, tga\_palette\_start);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5843             \textcolor{comment}{//   load the palette}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5844             tga\_palette = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad2(tga\_palette\_len, tga\_comp, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5845             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!tga\_palette) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5846                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5847                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5848             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5849             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_rgb16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5850                 stbi\_uc* pal\_entry = tga\_palette;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5851                 STBI\_ASSERT(tga\_comp == STBI\_rgb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5852                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_palette\_len; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5853                     stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(s, pal\_entry);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5854                     pal\_entry += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5855                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5856             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5857             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_getn(s, tga\_palette, tga\_palette\_len * tga\_comp)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5858                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5859                 STBI\_FREE(tga\_palette);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5860                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad palette"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt TGA"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5861             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5862         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5863         \textcolor{comment}{//   load the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5864         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_width * tga\_height; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5865         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5866             \textcolor{comment}{//   if I'm in RLE mode, do I need to get a RLE stbi\_\_pngchunk?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5867             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_is\_RLE)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5868             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5869                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (RLE\_count == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5870                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5871                     \textcolor{comment}{//   yep, get the next byte as a RLE command}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5872                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} RLE\_cmd = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5873                     RLE\_count = 1 + (RLE\_cmd \& 127);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5874                     RLE\_repeating = RLE\_cmd >> 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5875                     read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5876                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5877                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!RLE\_repeating)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5878                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5879                     read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5880                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5881             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5882             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5883             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5884                 read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5885             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5886             \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, if I need to read a pixel, do it now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5887             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (read\_next\_pixel)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5888             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5889                 \textcolor{comment}{//   load however much data we did have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5890                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_indexed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5891                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5892                     \textcolor{comment}{// read in index, then perform the lookup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5893                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pal\_idx = (tga\_bits\_per\_pixel == 8) ? stbi\_\_get8(s) : stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5894                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pal\_idx >= tga\_palette\_len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5895                         \textcolor{comment}{// invalid index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5896                         pal\_idx = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5897                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5898                     pal\_idx *= tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5899                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5900                         raw\_data[j] = tga\_palette[pal\_idx + j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5901                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5902                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5903                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_rgb16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5904                     STBI\_ASSERT(tga\_comp == STBI\_rgb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5905                     stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(s, raw\_data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5906                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5907                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5908                     \textcolor{comment}{//   read in the data raw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5909                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5910                         raw\_data[j] = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5911                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5912                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5913                 \textcolor{comment}{//   clear the reading flag for the next pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5914                 read\_next\_pixel = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5915             \} \textcolor{comment}{// end of reading a pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5916 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5917             \textcolor{comment}{// copy data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5918             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5919                 tga\_data[i * tga\_comp + j] = raw\_data[j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5920 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5921             \textcolor{comment}{//   in case we're in RLE mode, keep counting down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5922             -\/-\/RLE\_count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5923         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5924         \textcolor{comment}{//   do I need to invert the image?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5925         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_inverted)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5926         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5927             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j * 2 < tga\_height; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5928             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5929                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index1 = j * tga\_width * tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5930                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index2 = (tga\_height -\/ 1 -\/ j) * tga\_width * tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5931                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = tga\_width * tga\_comp; i > 0; -\/-\/i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5932                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5933                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_data[index1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5934                     tga\_data[index1] = tga\_data[index2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5935                     tga\_data[index2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5936                     ++index1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5937                     ++index2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5938                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5939             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5940         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5941         \textcolor{comment}{//   clear my palette, if I had one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5942         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_palette != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5943         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5944             STBI\_FREE(tga\_palette);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5945         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5946     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5947 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5948     \textcolor{comment}{// swap RGB -\/ if the source data was RGB16, it already is in the right order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5949     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_comp >= 3 \&\& !tga\_rgb16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5950     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5951         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* tga\_pixel = tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5952         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_width * tga\_height; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5953         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5954             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_pixel[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5955             tga\_pixel[0] = tga\_pixel[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5956             tga\_pixel[2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5957             tga\_pixel += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5958         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5959     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5960 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5961     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to target component count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5962     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != tga\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5963         tga\_data = stbi\_\_convert\_format(tga\_data, tga\_comp, req\_comp, tga\_width, tga\_height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5964 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5965     \textcolor{comment}{//   the things I do to get rid of an error message, and yet keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5966     \textcolor{comment}{//   Microsoft's C compilers happy... [8\string^(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5967     tga\_palette\_start = tga\_palette\_len = tga\_palette\_bits =}
\DoxyCodeLine{5968         tga\_x\_origin = tga\_y\_origin = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5969     STBI\_NOTUSED(tga\_palette\_start);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5970     \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5971     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5972 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5973 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5975 \textcolor{comment}{// *************************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5976 \textcolor{comment}{// Photoshop PSD loader -\/-\/ PD by Thatcher Ulrich, integration by Nicolas Schulz, tweaked by STB}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5986 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5987 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5988     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5989 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5990     count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5992         len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5993         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5994             \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5995         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5996         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5997             \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5998             len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5999             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6000             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6001             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6002                 *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6003                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6004                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6005             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6006         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6007         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6008             stbi\_uc   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6009             \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6010             \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6011             len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6012             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6013             val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6014             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6015             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6016                 *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6017                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6018                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6019             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6020         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6021     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6022 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6023     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6024 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6025 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6026 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_psd\_load(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info* ri, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bpc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6027 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6028     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6029     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channelCount, compression;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6030     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channel, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6031     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bitdepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6032     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6033     stbi\_uc* out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6034     STBI\_NOTUSED(ri);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6035 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6036     \textcolor{comment}{// Check identifier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6037     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get32be(s) != 0x38425053)   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}8BPS"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6038         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not PSD"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6040     \textcolor{comment}{// Check file type version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6041     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6042         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong version"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported version of PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6044     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip 6 reserved bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6045     stbi\_\_skip(s, 6);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6046 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6047     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the number of channels (R, G, B, A, etc).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6048     channelCount = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6049     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount < 0 || channelCount > 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6050         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong channel count"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported number of channels in PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6051 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6052     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the rows and columns of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6053     h = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6054     w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6055 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6056     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6057     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w > STBI\_MAX\_DIMENSIONS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Very large image (corrupt?)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6058 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6059     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6060     bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6061     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6062         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6063 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6064     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6065     \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6066     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6067     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6068     \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6069     \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6070     \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6071     \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6072     \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6073     \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6074     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6075         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6076 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6077     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6078     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6079 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6080     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6081     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6083     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6084     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6085 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6086     \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6087     \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6088     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6089     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6090     compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6091     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6092         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6093 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6094     \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6095     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6096         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6097 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6098     \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6099 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6100     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6101         out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(8, w, h, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6102         ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6103     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6104     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6105         out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w * h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6106 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6107     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6108     pixelCount = w * h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6110     \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6111     \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6112 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6113     \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6114     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6115         \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6116         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6117         \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6118         \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6119         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6120         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6121         \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6122 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6123         \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6124         \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6125         stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6126 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6127         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6128         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6129             stbi\_uc* p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6130 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6131             p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6132             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6133                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6134                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6135                     *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6136             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6137             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6138                 \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6139                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(s, p, pixelCount)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6140                     STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6141                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6142                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6143             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6144         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6145 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6146     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6147     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6148         \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6149         \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6150 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6151         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6152         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6153             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6154                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6155                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6156                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6157                     stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6158                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6159                         *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6160                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6161                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6162                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6163                     stbi\_uc val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6164                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6165                         *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6166                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6167             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6168             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6169                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6170                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6171                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6172                         *q = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6173                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6174                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6175                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6176                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6177                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6178                             *p = (stbi\_uc)(stbi\_\_get16be(s) >> 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6179                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6180                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6181                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6182                             *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6183                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6184                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6185             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6186         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6187     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6189     \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6190     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6191         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6192             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6193                 stbi\_\_uint16* pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16*)out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6194                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6195                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6196                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6197                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6198                     pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6199                     pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6200                     pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6201                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6202             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6203         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6204         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6205             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6206                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* pixel = out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6207                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6208                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6209                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6210                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6211                     pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6212                     pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6213                     pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6214                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6215             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6216         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6217     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6218 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6219     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to desired output format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6220     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6221         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6222             out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_convert\_format16((stbi\_\_uint16*)out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6223         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6224             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6225         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out == NULL) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_convert\_format frees input on failure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6226     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6227 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6228     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (comp) *comp = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6229     *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6230     *x = w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6231 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6232     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6233 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6605 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6606     lzw\_cs = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6607     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (lzw\_cs > 12) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6608     clear = 1 << lzw\_cs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6609     first = 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6612     bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6613     valid\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6614     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (init\_code = 0; init\_code < clear; init\_code++) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6631             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6633             bits |= (stbi\_\_int32)stbi\_\_get8(s) << valid\_bits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6634             valid\_bits += 8;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6642                 codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6643                 codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6650                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((len = stbi\_\_get8(s)) > 0)}

\DoxyCodeLine{6653             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6688 \textcolor{comment}{// this function is designed to support animated gifs, although stb\_image doesn't support it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6689 \textcolor{comment}{// two back is the image from two frames ago, used for a very specific disposal format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6690 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_gif\_load\_next(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_\_gif* g, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_uc* two\_back)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6691 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6692     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dispose;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6693     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} first\_frame;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6694     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pi;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6695     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pcount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6696     STBI\_NOTUSED(req\_comp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6697 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6698     \textcolor{comment}{// on first frame, any non-\/written pixels get the background colour (non-\/transparent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6699     first\_frame = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6700     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>out == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6701         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_gif\_header(s, g, comp, 0)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_g\_failure\_reason set by stbi\_\_gif\_header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6702         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, g-\/>w, g-\/>h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6703             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}GIF image is too large"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6704         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6705         g-\/>out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6706         g-\/>background = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6707         g-\/>history = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6708         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!g-\/>out || !g-\/>background || !g-\/>history)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6709             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6710 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6711         \textcolor{comment}{// image is treated as "{}transparent"{} at the start -\/ ie, nothing overwrites the current background;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6712         \textcolor{comment}{// background colour is only used for pixels that are not rendered first frame, after that "{}background"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6713         \textcolor{comment}{// color refers to the color that was there the previous frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6714         memset(g-\/>out, 0x00, 4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6715         memset(g-\/>background, 0x00, 4 * pcount); \textcolor{comment}{// state of the background (starts transparent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6716         memset(g-\/>history, 0x00, pcount);        \textcolor{comment}{// pixels that were affected previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6717         first\_frame = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6718     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6719     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6720         \textcolor{comment}{// second frame -\/ how do we dispose of the previous one?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6721         dispose = (g-\/>eflags \& 0x1C) >> 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6722         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6724         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((dispose == 3) \&\& (two\_back == 0)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6725             dispose = 2; \textcolor{comment}{// if I don't have an image to revert back to, default to the old background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6726         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6727 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6728         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dispose == 3) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// use previous graphic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6729             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (pi = 0; pi < pcount; ++pi) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6730                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>history[pi]) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6731                     memcpy(\&g-\/>out[pi * 4], \&two\_back[pi * 4], 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6732                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6733             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6734         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6735         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dispose == 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6736             \textcolor{comment}{// restore what was changed last frame to background before that frame;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6737             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (pi = 0; pi < pcount; ++pi) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6738                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>history[pi]) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6739                     memcpy(\&g-\/>out[pi * 4], \&g-\/>background[pi * 4], 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6740                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6741             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6742         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6743         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6744             \textcolor{comment}{// This is a non-\/disposal case eithe way, so just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6745             \textcolor{comment}{// leave the pixels as is, and they will become the new background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6746             \textcolor{comment}{// 1: do not dispose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6747             \textcolor{comment}{// 0:  not specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6748         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6750         \textcolor{comment}{// background is what out is after the undoing of the previou frame;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6751         memcpy(g-\/>background, g-\/>out, 4 * g-\/>w * g-\/>h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6752     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6753 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6754     \textcolor{comment}{// clear my history;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6755     memset(g-\/>history, 0x00, g-\/>w * g-\/>h);        \textcolor{comment}{// pixels that were affected previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6756 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6757     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6758         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} tag = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6759         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (tag) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6760         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0x2C: \textcolor{comment}{/* Image Descriptor */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6761         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6762             stbi\_\_int32 x, y, w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6763             stbi\_uc* o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6764 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6765             x = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6766             y = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6767             w = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6768             h = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6769             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((x + w) > (g-\/>w)) || ((y + h) > (g-\/>h)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6770                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad Image Descriptor"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6771 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6772             g-\/>line\_size = g-\/>w * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6773             g-\/>start\_x = x * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6774             g-\/>start\_y = y * g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6775             g-\/>max\_x = g-\/>start\_x + w * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6776             g-\/>max\_y = g-\/>start\_y + h * g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6777             g-\/>cur\_x = g-\/>start\_x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6778             g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>start\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6779 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6780             \textcolor{comment}{// if the width of the specified rectangle is 0, that means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6781             \textcolor{comment}{// we may not see *any* pixels or the image is malformed;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6782             \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure this is caught, move the current y down to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6783             \textcolor{comment}{// max\_y (which is what out\_gif\_code checks).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6784             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6785                 g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>max\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6786 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6787             g-\/>lflags = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6788 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6789             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>lflags \& 0x40) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6790                 g-\/>step = 8 * g-\/>line\_size; \textcolor{comment}{// first interlaced spacing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6791                 g-\/>parse = 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6792             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6793             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6794                 g-\/>step = g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6795                 g-\/>parse = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6796             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6797 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6798             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>lflags \& 0x80) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6799                 stbi\_\_gif\_parse\_colortable(s, g-\/>lpal, 2 << (g-\/>lflags \& 7), g-\/>eflags \& 0x01 ? g-\/>transparent : -\/1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6800                 g-\/>color\_table = (stbi\_uc*)g-\/>lpal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6801             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6802             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>flags \& 0x80) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6803                 g-\/>color\_table = (stbi\_uc*)g-\/>pal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6804             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6805             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6806                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}missing color table"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6808             o = stbi\_\_process\_gif\_raster(s, g);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6809             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!o) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6810 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6811             \textcolor{comment}{// if this was the first frame,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6812             pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6813             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (first\_frame \&\& (g-\/>bgindex > 0)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6814                 \textcolor{comment}{// if first frame, any pixel not drawn to gets the background color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6815                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (pi = 0; pi < pcount; ++pi) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6816                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>history[pi] == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6817                         g-\/>pal[g-\/>bgindex][3] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// just in case it was made transparent, undo that; It will be reset next frame if need be;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6818                         memcpy(\&g-\/>out[pi * 4], \&g-\/>pal[g-\/>bgindex], 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6819                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6820                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6821             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6822 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6823             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6824         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6825 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6826         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0x21: \textcolor{comment}{// Comment Extension.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6827         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6828             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6829             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ext = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6830             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ext == 0xF9) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// Graphic Control Extension.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6831                 len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6832                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6833                     g-\/>eflags = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6834                     g-\/>delay = 10 * stbi\_\_get16le(s); \textcolor{comment}{// delay -\/ 1/100th of a second, saving as 1/1000ths.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6835 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6836                     \textcolor{comment}{// unset old transparent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6837                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>transparent >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6838                         g-\/>pal[g-\/>transparent][3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6839                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6840                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>eflags \& 0x01) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6841                         g-\/>transparent = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6842                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>transparent >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6843                             g-\/>pal[g-\/>transparent][3] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6844                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6845                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6846                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6847                         \textcolor{comment}{// don't need transparent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6848                         stbi\_\_skip(s, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6849                         g-\/>transparent = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6850                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6851                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6852                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6853                     stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6854                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6855                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6856             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6857             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((len = stbi\_\_get8(s)) != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6858                 stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6859             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6860             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6861         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6862 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6863         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0x3B: \textcolor{comment}{// gif stream termination code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6864             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (stbi\_uc*)s; \textcolor{comment}{// using '1' causes warning on some compilers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6865 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6866         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6867             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unknown code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6868         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6869     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6872 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_load\_gif\_main(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}** delays, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* z, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6873 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6893                 *x = g.w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6894                 *y = g.h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6895                 ++layers;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6896                 stride = g.w * g.h * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6897 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6900                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (NULL == tmp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6901                         STBI\_FREE(g.out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6902                         STBI\_FREE(g.history);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6903                         STBI\_FREE(g.background);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6904                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6905                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6906                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6907                         out = (stbi\_uc*)tmp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6908                         out\_size = layers * stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6909                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6910 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6911                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delays) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6912                         *delays = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}*)STBI\_REALLOC\_SIZED(*delays, delays\_size, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) * layers);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6913                         delays\_size = layers * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(int);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6914                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6915                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6916                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6917                     out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(layers * stride);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6918                     out\_size = layers * stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6919                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delays) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6921                         delays\_size = layers * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(int);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6922                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6923                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6924                 memcpy(out + ((layers -\/ 1) * stride), u, stride);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6925                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (layers >= 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6926                     two\_back = out -\/ 2 * stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6927                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6928 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6929                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delays) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6931                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6932             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6933         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (u != 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6934 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6937         STBI\_FREE(g.history);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6938         STBI\_FREE(g.background);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6939 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6941         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6942             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, layers * g.w, g.h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6943 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6945         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6946     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6947     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6948         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not GIF"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Image was not as a gif type."{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6949     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{7036 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_hdr\_convert(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* output, stbi\_uc* input, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7037 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7038     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (input[3] != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7039         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7040         \textcolor{comment}{// Exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7041         f1 = (float)ldexp(1.0f, input[3] -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(128 + 8));}
\DoxyCodeLine{7042         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp <= 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7043             output[0] = (input[0] + input[1] + input[2]) * f1 / 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7044         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7045             output[0] = input[0] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7046             output[1] = input[1] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7047             output[2] = input[2] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7048         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7049         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 2) output[1] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7050         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 4) output[3] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7051     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7052     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7053         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (req\_comp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7054         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4: output[3] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7055         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3: output[0] = output[1] = output[2] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7056             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7057         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2: output[1] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7058         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1: output[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7059             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{7060         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7061     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7062 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7063 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7064 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* stbi\_\_hdr\_load(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info* ri)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7065 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{7066     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[STBI\_\_HDR\_BUFLEN];}
\DoxyCodeLine{7067     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* token;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7068     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} valid = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7069     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width, height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{7070     stbi\_uc* scanline;}

\DoxyCodeLine{7653 \textcolor{comment}{                         1-\/bit BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7654 \textcolor{comment}{                         *\_is\_16\_bit api}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7655 \textcolor{comment}{                         avoid warnings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7656 \textcolor{comment}{      2.16  (2017-\/07-\/23) all functions have 16-\/bit variants;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7657 \textcolor{comment}{                         STBI\_NO\_STDIO works again;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7658 \textcolor{comment}{                         compilation fixes;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7659 \textcolor{comment}{                         fix rounding in unpremultiply;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7660 \textcolor{comment}{                         optimize vertical flip;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7661 \textcolor{comment}{                         disable raw\_len validation;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7662 \textcolor{comment}{                         documentation fixes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7663 \textcolor{comment}{      2.15  (2017-\/03-\/18) fix png-\/1,2,4 bug; now all Imagenet JPGs decode;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7664 \textcolor{comment}{                         warning fixes; disable run-\/time SSE detection on gcc;}}
